<Review>A new Starbucks, a drive through, which is great. But omg, they are SLOW. Yesterday it took them a full 5 minutes to simply pour me a cup of dark drip coffee. As I sat at the window, already paid. I suppose they had to brew a pot to accomplish this? I finally hollered in that Pikes was fine, just hand me something!
The little girl who eventually showed up was all wiggles and smiles, we got your dark roast!!! So proud!!!
I'd give that a pass, but I have been going here a lot, and they are consistently off. Today, they were out of most breakfast sandwiches,  so I ordered the egg bites. 4 cars ahead of me at time of order. Get to window, get coffee, wait. Then asked to drive to the front so someone can bring out the egg bites. Wait another 6 minutes. Seriously? Then watched a young man roam from car to car, holding them out, did you order these? Apparently no one thought to identify my vehicle. And no, there was no one inside, and obviously no one ahead of me. A 30 second task required about 15 minutes to accomplish.

In addition, when getting a refill, the girl demanded my "Starbucks card" to scan for payment. I said no, I'm trying to hand you 50 cents. She stared at the coins , not moving,  apparently not comprehending.  All of this and more, after at least 10-15 visits, is what's happening here.

All delays were blamed on mistakes. Right. No kidding.

< text>
This place is nice and clean and the staff friendly. The one star rating is due to their corporate customer service and policies.  After a week I decided I wanted to put more in storage than I had originally planned. I called the location office to upgrade to a bigger unit. turns out, it isn't possible to upgrade a current (1 week in) unit. I have to get another unit with no move in discount plus still pay for the full month of the unit I've had a week. So basically pay for two units when I only needed 5 more feet of space.
I called the national customer service and was told the same thing. I explained that I'm trying to give them more money. They gave me the alternate choice to move out of my unit then get a different unit in 7 days. When I said this was horrible customer service the person asked if there was anything else they could do. I had to laugh. I said she could figure out how to make this work. She responded with "have a nice day" then hung up on me.
I called the new Extra Space just down the street. I had planned to move from an Extra Space location in LA to the Public Storage location as it was more convenient and their prices were good. Even though I'm an existing customer with Extra Space they still gave me a month free and will prorate the month at my old unit.
If Public Storage had figured out how to do this they would have had a customer for at least the next 2 years but now they've lost a customer forever.<//text>
